# Iteration Log: Pingis ML App

Date: 2026-04-24
Owner: Codex + Love
Scope: Collector app, audio review, racket/table/floor sound models, playing-mode retro audio, and video stroke review

## Purpose

This file is the working log for:
- APK builds
- model versions and metrics
- device feedback
- product decisions
- next steps

This is the project memory and handoff file for AI assistants.
For bounce/audio/ML work, read this file after the relevant Skill before making changes.
Do not move day-to-day model state into [AGENTS.md](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/AGENTS.md>); `AGENTS.md` should only point future agents here.

## Product Goal

The final goal is a full pingis training app that can:
- Collect data on-device with low friction.
- Record audio and video for review.
- Let the user review and correct labels in the app so training data is trustworthy.
- Pull collected sessions back to the computer.
- Run deterministic preprocessing and ML training locally.
- Track model quality over time.
- Export updated model artifacts into the React Native app.
- Install test APKs on the Motorola for live validation.

The immediate product goal is a stable audio-first bounce detector:
- It should reliably detect `racket_contact`.
- It should reject `floor_bounce`, `table_bounce`, speech, music, desk sounds, claps, clicks, and other hard transients.
- It should avoid double-counting one physical racket contact.
- It should work for straight-up racket bounces and for forehand/backhand-style racket contacts.

The longer-term product goal is audio/video fusion:
- Retro audio says whether the ball likely contacted the racket or table.
- Video pose says whether the selected player made a forehand/backhand-style stroke.
- When retro audio and video evidence agree after recording/import, the app can count in-play strokes with higher confidence.
- External IMU/AirHive work is no longer active product scope.

## System Workflow

1. Collect on Motorola in the app.
2. Review audio markers in the app; video is review support only, not a training input.
3. Pull `audio_session_*.json` and matching media folders from `/sdcard/Download/pingis_sessions` to [data/audio/raw](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/data/audio/raw>).
4. Preprocess with [preprocess_audio.py](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/skills/pingis-audio-classification/scripts/preprocess_audio.py>).
5. Build contact variants with [build_audio_contact_dataset_variant.py](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/skills/pingis-audio-classification/scripts/build_audio_contact_dataset_variant.py>), reporting `human_reviewed` separately from weak legacy/bootstrap variants.
6. Train the binary model with [train_rf_audio_contact.py](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/skills/pingis-audio-classification/scripts/train_rf_audio_contact.py>).
7. Train the 4-class model with [train_rf_audio.py](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/skills/pingis-audio-classification/scripts/train_rf_audio.py>).
8. Export app artifacts with [export_contact_model_json.py](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/skills/pingis-audio-classification/scripts/export_contact_model_json.py>) and [export_model_json.py](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/skills/pingis-audio-classification/scripts/export_model_json.py>).
9. Build and install the Android release APK locally before trusting live behavior.

## Current Focus

Audio quality and reviewed ground truth are the priority. Current model work is split into `studs_live`, `spel_retro_audio`, and `video_stroke_model`; keep those scopes separate.

T0029 review-start performance work resumed after T0033 parity. T0030 used `audio_session_2026-06-04_006` to train a better `spel_retro_audio` model, and T0031 installed that model on Motorola. T0032 same-clip audit showed the installed app saved `130 TP / 0 wrong / 0 FP / 9 missed` against the 139-marker `006` truth while Python replay expected `133 / 0 / 0 / 6`. T0033 reproduced the app output locally with Collector TypeScript features plus app gates, so future promotion must use app-style output replay. T0034-T0036 are local app changes: timing visibility, pose deferral, and exact-output runtime cleanup.

Separate experiment: `Video stroke test` is allowed as an Android-only branch for camera-based forehand/backhand classification. It must keep its data under `/Download/pingis_video_stroke_sessions` and `data/video/*` so it does not affect the audio detector or audio review training data.
Current video-only experiment: `Video FH/BH` imports one MP4, extracts embedded audio to WAV only for waveform review, runs ML Kit pose at 15 fps, proposes whole-video motion markers with the current video-stroke model, and saves confirmed markers as `video_stroke_session_*.json` for offline retraining. Review v5 mirrors the normal audio review controls as closely as this video-only flow allows: audible source audio, WAV timeline, zoom through 16x, robust playhead/timeline drag and long-press marker creation, previous/next marker nav, marker utility controls including +/-50 ms, and selected `-700/+500 ms` stroke playback.
New T0037 experiment: `Video studs FH/BH` imports one MP4, extracts embedded audio to WAV, finds audio-peak bounce anchors, and labels the racket side at impact as FH-side, BH-side, or unknown. It saves under `/Download/pingis_video_bounce_side_sessions` as `video_bounce_side_session_*.json` with `collection_type=video_bounce_side_snapshot`. This is not the same as stroke-motion FH/BH. T0037 was installed on Motorola `ZY22L6NDHV` on 2026-06-09 with APK SHA256 `C445A5B66901A668C8EB0EF0413F8E42323531FF3A8EE6F31093D4F1FA9C87C3`. T0038 pulled `_001`: 37 confirmed markers (`22 forehand`, `14 backhand`, `1 unknown`) with tight audio anchors. T0039 pulled `_002`-`_004`: `39 forehand`, `40 backhand`, and mixed `12 forehand` / `13 backhand` / `1 unknown`; combined `_001`-`_004` has `140` binary labels plus `2` unknown. T0040 tested local ROI classifiers: broad/fixed ROI did not work on the mixed `_004` holdout, but a tight red-anchor racket-side ROI reached `0.92` accuracy on train `_002`+`_003` -> test mixed `_004` with confusion matrix `[[11, 1], [1, 12]]`. That is a real positive signal, not app-ready proof; next step is one fresh mixed holdout and a robust app-side ROI before export.
T0041 responded to live `Studs FH/BH LIVE` feedback from 2026-06-17: the installed Fable v5 APK was detecting racket-bounce audio, but side resolution was almost all `backhand` even when debug crops visibly showed red racket evidence. The fix keeps Fable and `bounce_side_model.json` unchanged, adds a runtime visible-color resolver for red/black evidence, and installs a new APK so red-forehand tests should no longer collapse to all backhand. T0042 added the continuous live racket box/color tracker; T0043 then hardened black-side tracking after device feedback showed hair and black shirts could be labeled `racket-black`, added a close-up compact-rubber exception after a live screenshot showed the first hardened gate rejected a real black racket, and added a 95% visible-box/side-decision confidence gate after racket-absent false boxes. T0044 paused further camera-side changes to add evaluation-only Fable tooling, T0045 ran that tooling on real TT Sounds, T0046 pulled/evaluated available Motorola artifacts, T0047 pulled Love's fresh home-practice Fable debug validation plus retest rounds, T0048 decoded/audited the exact app-domain snippets, and T0049 tried the approved June 28 clips as a tiny speech-veto candidate. T0050 then pulled Love's targeted Fable-algoritm round and evaluated all saved debug events for the mapped A/B/C blocks. Result: the current Fable app count is not reliable enough for the kid/home-practice target without more audio work (`196` mapped real racket contacts expected vs `132` counted, plus `5` false counts on negative blocks). Love confirmed C2 was valid hard-mode practice, but the stitched event snippets were discontinuous and missed some real bounce sounds. T0051 added continuous WAV capture to `Fable-algoritm` debug. T0052 pulled the first continuous C2-style run after that install: expected/app was `30/0`, saved JSON had `48` native candidates, and `44` classified candidates were rejected as `noise`/`not_racket`. T0053 added a local browser UI at `http://127.0.0.1:8765/` so Love can play the WAV, inspect the 48 candidates, label them, and add missed manual markers before retrain/replay. T0054 made that UI timestamp-review friendly with draggable markers, adjusted trigger times, original-time preservation, and playhead-based playback. T0055 ingested Love's saved labels: `30` racket contacts and `19` noise labels; `29` reviewed racket labels were attached to saved phone-trigger rows, but many were manually time-adjusted, so this is not exact native-hit coverage. T0056 then checked exact saved app clips, raw/native recuts, corrected timestamps, and local peak recentering: exact saved app clips were `29/29` noise, corrected timestamps were only `2/30` racket, peak recentering did not help, and T0049-only candidates still failed C2. T0057 added a repeatable local improvement loop: best fast candidate `rf_fast_balanced` on `t0049_plus_c2` at threshold `0.7` gives exact C2 `18` TP / `0` FP / `12` missed and reduces T0050 negative false counts from `5` to `1`, but it uses C2 in training and has no 4-class table/floor safety. T0058 added optional held-out WAV/count replay plus capped TT Sounds safety diagnostics. A tiny TT sample showed `11/15` non-racket positives (`5/5` floor, `5/5` table, `1/5` noise), so the candidate is clearly not export-ready. T0059 made local reviewed discovery recursive and confirmed the local reviewed pull only has `44` racket positives and `0` local table/floor/noise safety negatives. T0060 pulled Love's fresh held-out C2-like run (`31` expected, app `1`), confirmed `59` native candidates and `1` counted event, and showed the best diagnostic candidate also counted only `1/31` on the held-out WAV. T0061/T0062 created a faster manual-only timestamp UI for that T0060 WAV, and T0063 ingested Love's saved `31` manual racket labels. Exact current-only replay of the bundled Fable path counted `7` with `5 TP / 2 FP / 26 missed`; centered on Love's labels, the current model predicted `17/31` racket and only `5/31` cleared threshold. T0064 added a separate app DATA recorder so Love can collect focused continuous WAVs with scenario labels and expected counts/unclear metadata. T0065 pulled Round A (`34` clips plus one smoke test) and count-replayed the current bundled Fable path: positives counted `810/965`, negatives false-counted `164/0`, with clean/slow/fast/messy count-close but background-sound positives and handling/floor-table-other negatives still poor. T0066 reviewed all four background-sound clips into `196` exact contacts. T0067 then showed a simple strict peak gate can recover those peaks but peak-only is unsafe and the strict `380 ms` cooldown misses fast racket (`97/135`). T0068 compared current RMS/native candidate generation to peak variants: `Peak fast balanced` reached exact recall `1.000` versus RMS `0.714`, reduced selected hard-negative candidates `1025 -> 358`, improved median timing `31.0 ms -> 1.5 ms`, and covered fast racket `136/135`. The next audio step is peak candidate generator plus speech/noise/impact veto or classifier and app-style safety replay before any export/build, with RMS kept as fallback until that full chain passes.
`Ljud + video ML` remains staged, but Review 2 now follows the same whole-video FH/BH motion review pattern as `Video FH/BH`: audio Review 1 stays normal, pose scans the full MP4 at 15 fps in the background, and motion markers are reviewed separately from audio markers.

The audio work should continue training both:
- 4-class `audio_model`, because it is the current default live count engine in `Normal / 4-klass`.
- Binary `audio_contact_model`, because it remains useful for debug/comparison and optional hybrid mode.

Current binary training strategy:
- Human-reviewed markers are the single source of truth.
- Legacy data is allowed only as weak/bootstrap coverage and must be reported separately from `human_reviewed`.
- Reports must compare source/trust, scenario, FH/BH prompt metadata, hard-negative kind, and live-chain replay before exporting a new APK model.
- New training/export work must not reintroduce external IMU/AirHive assumptions unless Love explicitly reopens that scope.

## Current Known Problems

| Area | Symptom | Current interpretation | Next diagnostic |
|---|---|---|---|
| Double count | One racket bounce plus catching/after-sound can become two counted contacts | Likely live onset/merge-window/timing behavior, not only model quality | Inspect debug rows: counted vs `merge_window`; consider stronger merge after a counted contact |
| Speech false positives | T0050 negative blocks false-counted talking/handling: B1 `1/0`, B3 `3/0`, B4 `1/0` | T0049/T0050 confirm confidence-only and tiny veto gates are not enough; the partial veto catches too little and can reject real bounces | Use speech/racket-handling hard negatives in a full retrain/replay candidate, not a quick threshold-only gate |
| Messy-practice recall | T0050 mapped real blocks counted only `132/196`; T0052 continuous C2-style run counted `0/30`; T0060 fresh held-out run counted `1/31`; T0063 exact current-only replay counted `7` with `5 TP / 2 FP / 26 missed`; T0065 Round A count-level positives replayed `810/965`; T0066 reviewed background positives show current app/replay counted only `55/196` exact labels; T0068 `Peak fast balanced` candidate gate reached `196/196` exact background recall and `136/135` fast Round A candidates | T0055 labels confirm `30` racket contacts and `19` noise labels. T0056 shows timing/window alignment is not enough. T0063 shows current Fable is weak even when centered on Love's corrected labels (`17/31` racket, only `5/31` above threshold) and native/gate timing also contributes (`19/31` labels within `140 ms`, `27/31` within `250 ms`). T0065 shows count-close behavior for normal/slow/fast/messy but major recall loss for background-sound positives (`55/200`) and major false-counts for hard negatives (`164` total). T0068 shows peak candidate generation can beat RMS/native on exact recall, timing, fast coverage, and hard-negative candidate load, but final counting still needs classifier/veto and dedupe. | Peak-candidate generator plus speech/noise/impact veto or classifier and app-style replay before any model export/build |
| Missed angled contacts | Forehand/backhand-style contacts are missed more often than straight vertical bounces | Training data is biased toward vertical racket bounces; live onset may also miss lower or angled transients | Collect reviewed `racket_forehand_bounce` and `racket_backhand_bounce` style takes or fold this into prompts |
| Floor false positives | Floor bounces have historically been counted as racket contacts | Improved but not solved; latest 4-class `floor_bounce` recall is only 0.61 | More floor data in multiple positions/surfaces plus verify whether veto sees `floor_bounce` live |
| Video/audio offset | Auto sync can pick the wrong sound when another transient happens before the clap | Manual audio-anchor plus exact video-frame sync is now implemented for review; persistence still needs Motorola validation | Device-test with a misleading early sound, set `Sätt ljudsync här` + `Synka här`, save, reopen, and verify the same anchors |

## Current Decisions

| Date | Decision | Why |
|---|---|---|
| 2026-06-29 | Use `Peak fast balanced` as the next primary candidate-gate candidate, keep RMS fallback | T0068 directly compared RMS/native versus peak candidate gates. `Peak fast balanced` reached exact recall `1.000`, selected hard-negative candidates `358`, median timing `1.5 ms`, and fast `136/135`, versus current RMS/native exact recall `0.714`, selected hard-negative candidates `1025`, median timing `31.0 ms`, and fast `151/135`. This is candidate evidence only; final app behavior still needs classifier/veto and dedupe replay. |
| 2026-06-29 | Use waveform peaks as candidate generator, not standalone counter | T0067 best peak gate recovered `192/196` exact reviewed background-sound contacts versus current Fable `41/196`, but broad Round A replay false-counted talking-only `130` and missed fast racket (`97/135`). It needs speech/noise/impact veto or classifier plus dynamic cooldown before runtime use. |
| 2026-06-29 | Treat Round A as high-value recorder evidence, not event-level training truth yet | T0065 has strong scenario/count metadata, but positive clips only have total expected contacts. The current replay is count-level: useful for scenario diagnosis, not enough to know which exact windows should be positive training rows. Exact timestamp review or a row-generation plan is needed before retraining/export. |
| 2026-06-29 | Use a separate Fable data recorder before retraining/export | T0063 showed the current Fable path is weak on the hard self-practice domain, but the biggest bottleneck is still balanced, well-described local WAVs. T0064 collects full continuous audio plus scenario/count metadata without changing live counting, camera, model JSON, or thresholds. |
| 2026-06-29 | Do not export/build after T0063 exact T0060 replay | Current-only replay of the bundled Fable path against Love's `31` exact labels counted only `7` with `5 TP / 2 FP / 26 missed`; centered labels were only `17/31` racket and `5/31` above threshold, while gate timing only matched `19/31` within `140 ms`. |
| 2026-06-17 | Guard the bounce-side model with visible racket color before retraining | Today's live dumps showed correct Fable audio anchors but raw side predictions collapsing to backhand on visibly red crops. Because TS parity passed, the immediate safe fix is runtime color resolution and richer debug fields; a future retrain can still use the collected failures. |
| 2026-06-09 | Use tight racket-side ROI for the first bounce-side detector path | T0040 showed broad/full body crops are near chance on mixed holdout, while tight racket-side evidence gives a strong current-data signal. The approach still needs a fresh mixed holdout and app-side ROI robustness before export. |
| 2026-06-09 | Start bounce-side video as audio-anchored snapshot labels | Love wants side classification at the bounce instant. Current pose can track wrist but may not expose palm/racket roll, so collect real FH-side/BH-side/unknown examples first and decide in T0038 whether pose-only is enough or Hand Landmarker is needed |
| 2026-06-01 | Keep 06-01 Tomas backhand retrain out of the app | The new trainable backhand session improves its own dense replay, but it adds false positives on existing Tomas/Stiga sessions and one extra false positive on ordinary 05-13 normal replay; ordinary up/down must remain unaffected |
| 2026-06-01 | Hide non-review-relevant audio candidates in normal Review | Transparent blue table candidates looked like deleted/untouchable markers even though they are only saved analysis candidates; normal Review should show editable truth and relevant suggestions, not every hidden debug candidate |
| 2026-05-29 | Use staged whole-video motion review for `Ljud + video ML` | Love wants the normal audio review first, then a `Video FH/BH`-style Review 2 that scans the whole MP4 and reviews separate FH/BH/Oklart motion markers rather than only checking confirmed audio racket hits |
| 2026-05-25 | Use `Hoppa över ljud` for video-only pose review | The separate `Videoinsamling FH/BH` flow is removed; imported videos now use `Ljud + video ML`, and if audio is not useful the review runs pose over the whole video instead of requiring audio anchors |
| 2026-05-28 | Use `Video FH/BH` for camera-only data collection | Video-only FH/BH needs a cleaner workflow than `Ljud + video ML`: one visible player, required handedness/camera-side metadata, 15 fps pose, and reviewed markers saved directly to the video-stroke training format |
| 2026-05-28 | Ask for audio intake metadata before training new files | New audio can belong to ordinary bounce, dense playing, Stiga/Tomas hard stroke sounds, or diagnostic/holdout buckets; Codex must ask Love for missing bucket, impact, environment, device/player, and trainability metadata before preprocessing/training |
| 2026-05-29 | Keep 05-29 Tomas hard audio retrain out of the app | The new trainable session is useful domain data, but the 05-29 retrain adds false positives faster than true positives in live replay, so the installed 05-28 audio model remains better for now |
| 2026-05-28 | Build Tomas audio C APK for gated live validation | The candidate improves replay, but Tomas 28/5 is included in training and fast config still adds false positives, so the APK is built but not installed until Love approves Motorola testing |
| 2026-05-19 | Use two synchronized timelines for `Ljud + video ML` review | Audio hits and pose motions need to be reviewed as separate training layers while staying visually aligned in time |
| 2026-05-19 | Manual sync and two-layer labels in `Ljud + video ML` | Noisy recordings need a human-set clap in both audio and video, and audio training rows must stay separate from pose-motion training rows even when the UI visually links them |
| 2026-05-18 | Split one long video stroke source into 30 s review takes | Avoids fragile sequential 30 s recording/playback while preserving the existing review/training JSON shape for longer colleague/player sessions |
| 2026-05-19 | Keep audio and pose candidates separate in unified review | A hit can be useful audio truth, motion truth, or both; linked review markers make the UI readable while preserving separate rows for audio/contact and pose-motion training |
| 2026-05-22 | Store camera side separately from camera angle | `camera_angle=front_oblique` is not enough: `player_left` vs `player_right` changes the 2D pose feature distribution and must be tracked for balancing, evaluation, and later normalization |
| 2026-05-18 | Allow video stroke resume/import | Prevents losing long match recordings from the app workflow when the review screen is closed or the video already exists elsewhere on the phone |
| 2026-05-18 | Treat video stroke as data collection UI | Love expects it in the collection/data area and wants review ergonomics to follow the existing audio/video review, including playback speed |
| 2026-05-18 | Add separate Android video stroke test | Love wants a controlled front/snett-framifrån camera experiment to distinguish forehand/backhand motion; keep it separate from audio and IMU pipelines |
| 2026-05-11 | Add detection config, candidate, and review-truth layers | Love needs to see what the algorithm proposed and what was corrected without training on unreviewed auto detections; full model retraining remains offline |
| 2026-05-13 | Match app inference windows to tight model exports | Tight-trained audio models must classify the same `-60/+140 ms` event window in Review and Live; longer preview clips remain only for human listening |
| 2026-05-13 | Do not ship tight live inference until full-chain replay passes | Motorola testing showed tight live missed too many quiet racket bounces and could count speech at sensitive thresholds, despite strong marker-window/holdout metrics |
| 2026-05-13 | Human-reviewed markers are the single source of truth | Legacy rows can be useful for coverage, but they must stay explicitly marked as weak/bootstrap and never silently define final truth |
| 2026-05-13 | Use full live-chain replay before exporting the next Collector audio model | Stiga's better live behavior is mostly candidate/onset/gate behavior, not just a better model JSON |
| 2026-05-11 | Do not train on `audio_session_2026-05-11_001` | Love explicitly marked this session as diagnostic-only |
| 2026-05-11 | Allow `audio_session_2026-05-11_002` in training | Love explicitly marked both music takes as trainable |
| 2026-05-12 | Skip unfinished review-required takes in preprocessing | New takes can exist in a session before Love has reviewed them; they must not fall back to legacy auto-training |
| 2026-05-12 | Export the 2026-05-12 audio model pair | Today's reviewed noisy hard negatives improved the 4-class model and gave a stronger binary contact candidate than the active app artifact |
| 2026-05-12 | Do not export the first high-music-only retrain candidate | `audio_session_2026-05-12_004` adds useful coverage, but one high-music racket take is not enough to improve overall validation metrics |
| 2026-05-12 | Do not export the sessions 005/006 retrain candidate automatically | New iPhone/imported and high-music data is useful, but the candidate improves selected classes while weakening the overall validation balance; keep it as a local comparison model |
| 2026-05-13 | Do not export the first 009/010/011 tight candidate | The model trained successfully, but 011 exposed that the fixed 300 ms negative-overlap skip removes many real table bounces in dense table/racket sequences; preprocessing should skip only true window overlap before this data is used fully |
| 2026-05-13 | Replace fixed 300 ms negative skip with true training-window overlap | Dense play has legitimate table/racket gaps below 300 ms; with tight `-60/+140 ms` windows, those examples should train unless their actual extracted windows overlap |
| 2026-05-25 | Do not replace the installed dense CJ audio model from marker-window metrics alone | Latest dense session marker windows are already classified perfectly by the installed model; missing review/live events are mainly candidate threshold and close-event recovery issues |
| 2026-05-25 | `Känslig` must control the audio-video-pose review threshold | A hard 65% floor made sensitive Review generate nearly the same racket auto-markers as normal; audio-video-pose review now uses the selected config threshold instead |
| 2026-04-22 | Keep audio as the primary contact truth | It already works better than other paths and has real reviewed data |
| 2026-04-22 | Do not replace audio with IMU | IMU bounce work should be additive and removable |
| 2026-04-22 | If IMU is added, make it a separate bounce-specific model | Bounce motion is not the same as a normal pingis swing |
| 2026-04-22 | Keep audio review as the label source even in synced collection mode | One reviewed timeline should supervise both audio and IMU training |
| 2026-04-22 | Use `0.5-1.0 s` spacing between bounces in the base collection round | Keeps reviewed clips clean and easier to label |
| 2026-04-22 | Postpone fast double-bounce collection | Base review and base contact model are not stable enough yet |
| 2026-04-22 | Compare binary contact variants with legacy inclusion before shipping a new APK | We needed evidence, not guesses, about whether old 4-class data should feed the binary model |
| 2026-04-22 | Prefer `all_legacy` over current binary contact dataset for the next audio APK candidate | It is the first local binary variant that raises noisy positive recall without collapsing completely on negatives |
| 2026-04-23 | Keep IMU work paused and prioritize audio data plus audio model updates | New audio round materially improved negative recall and gave enough evidence to justify another audio-only test APK |
| 2026-04-24 | Treat review video as labeling support, not model input | The current ML pipeline trains from WAV features and review markers; adding video to ML would create a new problem before audio is stable |
| 2026-04-24 | Keep training the 4-class model even though binary is primary | Table/floor/noise separation is useful for live veto/debug and may become product behavior later |
| 2026-05-04 | Default contact training to human-reviewed markers | Prevents algorithm-proposed events from becoming final truth without review |
| 2026-05-04 | Keep legacy data as opt-in variants | Existing data is valuable for bootstrap/comparison but weaker than explicit review labels |
| 2026-05-04 | Split racket-bounce prompts from FH/BH labels | FH/BH is coverage and IMU-side metadata for bounce, not a separate audio class |
| 2026-05-04 | Keep bounce IMU and stroke IMU separate | Repeated racket-bounce motion and in-play stroke motion should not be trained as one task |
| 2026-05-06 | Use natural racket-arm motion as bounce-IMU negative data | Fake no-ball bounce rhythm is too similar to real racket bouncing and would create ambiguous IMU ground truth |
| 2026-05-04 | Prefer 150 Hz raw IMU collection when stable | Higher-resolution raw data can be downsampled later; measured rate and quality flags decide whether a take is trustworthy |
| 2026-05-04 | Hide old pending review samples from collection | Love should only see current-session pending work while collecting new takes; old samples are preserved on disk |
| 2026-05-04 | Use a clap/tap sync event for review video calibration | The saved `audio_origin_in_video_ms` is a good default, but Love needs a visible and audible anchor that can compute `video_sync_offset_ms` without guessing direction |
| 2026-05-05 | Hide legacy `Datainsamling` from startsida | It points to older IMU-only collection; keep the route/code as internal fallback while showing only active user-facing collection flows |
| 2026-05-05 | Move `Playing` under `Audio plus IMU` | Longer free play capture is a scenario for synced audio/video/IMU review, not a separate top-level home card |
| 2026-05-05 | Make FH/BH pose calibration optional after table baseline | Pose calibration is helper metadata; raw IMU should still be collected with `calibration_status: partial` if poses are skipped |

## Open Questions

| Date | Question | Current answer |
|---|---|---|
| 2026-04-22 | Is review UI simple enough to trust labeling? | Not fully confirmed yet |
| 2026-04-22 | Should the next implementation be synchronized audio + IMU collection? | Done |
| 2026-04-22 | Is the current binary audio model strong enough to preserve? | Yes |
| 2026-04-22 | Is synced review usable enough to start collecting bounce IMU data? | Not verified yet |
| 2026-04-22 | Should trusted legacy only be enough for binary contact? | No, not on the current local corpus; it is far too small and too positive-heavy |
| 2026-04-24 | Is the audio model stable enough for app-level bounce counting? | Not yet; duplicate counts and missed angled FH/BH contacts remain |
| 2026-04-24 | Is the next data gap more floor/table negatives or angled racket positives? | Both matter; current feedback says angled FH/BH contacts are under-covered and floor remains weak |
| 2026-05-04 | Should FH/BH racket-bounce be separate audio classes? | No; keep one audio contact label and store FH/BH as prompt/IMU-side metadata |
| 2026-05-04 | Should legacy data remain in the real model path? | Yes as opt-in variants, but primary metrics should report human-reviewed performance separately |

## Current Collection Checklist

Date: 2026-05-12

Goal: strengthen the audio models with noisy hard negatives and noisy racket positives. Use `Ljudinsamling` for all rows in this checklist; review each take before it is used for training.

| Priority | Scenario to record | Target | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---:|---|---|
| 1 | `Brus/negativt` with loud music or whistling | 3 x 30 s | Done | Pulled as `audio_session_2026-05-12_001`; 66 reviewed `not_racket_contact` / `voice_music_noise` markers are ready for the next training run |
| 2 | `Golvstuds stökigt` | 3 x 30 s | Partial | `audio_session_2026-05-12_002` has 2 reviewed takes with 59 `floor_bounce` markers; record 1 more take |
| 3 | `Bordsstuds stökigt` | 2-3 x 30 s | Pending | Bounce on a real ping-pong table or table-like playing surface, not an arbitrary desk |
| 4 | `Racket + hög musik` | 3 x 30 s | Partial | `audio_session_2026-05-12_004` has 1 reviewed `music_high` take with 40 racket contacts; record 2 more takes |
| 5 | `Racket + prat` | 1-2 x 30 s | Optional | `audio_session_2026-05-11_005` already gives useful corrected speech data; add more only if voice/distance/noise differs |
| 6 | `Brus/negativt` speech-only or music-only without ball impacts | 2 x 30 s | Optional | Useful if the app creates false peaks; label as `Brus`, not `Annat` |

Review rules for this round:
- Confirm or edit real racket, table, floor, and noise events; human-reviewed markers are the only training truth.
- Use `Brus` for music, speech, whistle, and phone noise.
- Use `Ignorera` for ambiguous overlaps near a real racket hit instead of forcing a negative label.
- Do not collect IMU for table, floor, or noise in this audio-only checklist.

## AI Handoff Checklist

When another AI assistant starts work on this project:
1. Read [AGENTS.md](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/AGENTS.md>).
2. Load relevant Skills, especially [pingis-audio-classification](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/skills/pingis-audio-classification/SKILL.md>) for audio work and [pingis-stroke-detection](</C:/Users/lovea/Desktop/dev/STIGA SPORTS/pingis_ml_algo/skills/pingis-stroke-detection/SKILL.md>) for IMU work.
3. Read this `ITERATION_LOG.md` before changing collector, review, model scripts, or live bounce logic.
4. Be critical: compare model variants with grouped splits, inspect scenario breakdowns, and do not assume more data automatically means a better live model.
5. Keep audio as the active priority until the known audio problems are resolved on device.
6. Update this file after every meaningful data pull, retrain, APK build, or device feedback round.

## How To Update This File

After each meaningful round, update at least:
1. `Metric History`
2. `Build History`
3. `Data Collection History`
4. one row in `Entry Log`

If a decision changes, update `Current Decisions` instead of burying it in free text.
